6c:["$","span","span-10",{"data-line":"","children":[["$","span","span-0",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#24292E","--shiki-dark":"#ABB2BF"},"children":"                <"}],["$","span","span-1",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#22863A","--shiki-dark":"#E06C75"},"children":"ui:Label"}],["$","span","span-2",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#6F42C1","--shiki-dark":"#D19A66"},"children":" text"}],["$","span","span-3",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#24292E","--shiki-dark":"#ABB2BF"},"children":"="}],["$","span","span-4",{"style":{"--shiki-light":"#032F62","--shiki-dark":"#98C379"},"children":"\"我不敢苟同。我个人认为这个意大利面就应该拌 42 号混凝土。因为这个螺丝钉的长度，它很容易会直接影响到挖掘机的扭距，你往里砸的时候，一瞬间它就会产生大量的高能蛋白，俗称 UFO。会严重影响经济的发展。照你这么说，炸鸡块要用
